\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01290}01290\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Inflating\ a\ polytope,\ idea\ by\ Dirk\ Gregorius\ \string~\ 2015.\ Works\ in\ both\ 2D\ and\ 3D.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01291}01291\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Reference:\ Halfspace\ intersection\ with\ Qhull\ by\ Brad\ Barber}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01292}01292\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ http://www.geom.uiuc.edu/graphics/pix/Special\_Topics/Computational\_Geometry/half.html}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01293}01293\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01294}01294\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Algorithm\ steps:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01295}01295\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 1.\ Find\ a\ point\ within\ the\ input\ poly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01296}01296\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 2.\ Center\ this\ point\ onto\ the\ origin.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01297}01297\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 3.\ Adjust\ the\ planes\ by\ a\ skin\ factor.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01298}01298\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 4.\ Compute\ the\ dual\ vert\ of\ each\ plane.\ Each\ plane\ becomes\ a\ vertex.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01299}01299\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ c2v\ dual(c2h\ plane)\ \{\ return\ c2V(plane.n.x\ /\ plane.d,\ plane.n.y\ /\ plane.d)\ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01300}01300\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 5.\ Compute\ the\ convex\ hull\ of\ the\ dual\ verts.\ This\ is\ called\ the\ dual.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01301}01301\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 6.\ Compute\ the\ dual\ of\ the\ dual,\ this\ will\ be\ the\ poly\ to\ return.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cute__c2_8h_source_l01302}01302\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 7.\ Translate\ the\ poly\ away\ from\ the\ origin\ by\ the\ center\ point\ from\ step\ 2.}}
